Coaches program 12-week strength plans, track client form, and send notes. Users log sets, view progress, and get automatically guided to their next session. The product is pre-scaffold but not yet feature-complete — agents are building it batch by batch via the `/monitor/roadmap` kickoff system.\n    17→\n    18→## Data Flow\n    19→\n    20→```\n    21→Browser ──► proxy.ts (auth guard + PIN gate + Supabase session refresh)\n    22→         ──► App Router server components (lib/supabase/server.ts)\n    23→         ──► Supabase PostgreSQL (RLS enforced)\n    24→\n    25→Monitor ──► /monitor/roadmap (server component, reads GitHub PR status + Upstash KV)\n    26→         ──► KickoffButton → POST /api/monitor/kickoff\n    27→         ──► GitHub workflow_dispatch → claude-feature.yml\n    28→         ──► Claude Code agent (reads GitHub Issue for spec, writes code, commits, pushes)\n    29→         ──► PR marked ready → human reviews + merges\n    30→```\n    31→\n    32→## Tech Stack\n    33→\n    34→| Layer | Technology |\n    35→|---|---|\n    36→| Framework | Next.js 16.2.2 — App Router, `proxy.ts` (not `middleware.ts`) |\n    37→| UI | React 19, Tailwind v4 (CSS-first), shadcn/ui v4 (base-nova style) |\n    38→| Auth + DB | Supabase (PostgreSQL + RLS + SSR auth via `@supabase/ssr`) |\n    39→| KV store | Upstash Redis (`@upstash/redis`) — roadmap status overrides only |\n    40→| Charts | Recharts |\n    41→| Animation | Framer Motion |\n    42→| DnD | dnd-kit (Batch 7) |\n    43→| Toast | Sonner |\n    44→| Server state | TanStack React Query |\n    45→| Client state | Zustand |\n    46→| Tests | Vitest + jsdom |\n    47→| CI | GitHub Actions — `claude-feature.yml` (agent) + `ci.yml` (lint/test) |\n    48→| Hosting | Vercel (auto-deploy `main`; preview on all branches) |\n    49→| Package mgr | pnpm 9 |\n    50→\n    51→## Key Files\n    52→\n    53→| File | Purpose |\n    54→|---|---|\n    55→| `proxy.ts` | Auth guard + monitor PIN gate + Supabase session refresh. {"type":"user","message":{"role":"user","content":[{"tool_use_id":"toolu_0113dSivJndVFxtwjcuFjYqN","type":"tool_result","content":"     1→---\n     2→type: gotchas\n     3→tags: [gotchas, lessons-learned, buildbase]\n     4→last-updated: 2026-04-16\n     5→---\n     6→\n     7→# Gotchas — BuildBase\n     8→\n     9→> Read this before starting any task. Each entry is a real thing that burned us.\n    10→> Add new entries at the top with the date.\n    11→\n    12→---\n    13→\n    14→## 2026-04-24 — Test files with JSX must use .tsx extension\n    15→\n    16→**Symptom:** `pnpm tsc --noEmit` fails with dozens of `'>' expected`, `',' expected`, and `Expression expected` errors in test files.\n    17→\n    18→**Cause:** TypeScript cannot parse JSX syntax (`<Component />`) in `.ts` files. The file must have a `.tsx` extension for JSX to be valid. This has burned us on items 3-2 and 3-3 — both times the agent wrote React component render tests in a `.ts` file.\n    19→\n    20→**Rule for test files:**\n    21→- If a test **imports and renders React components** (uses `render()`, JSX, `screen.*`) → name it `*.test.tsx`\n    22→- If a test **only tests pure functions, data transforms, and logic** (no JSX) → name it `*.test.ts`\n    23→\n    24→Most BuildBase tests should be `.test.ts` because coverage targets `lib/**/*.ts` (pure logic). Prefer testing the logic the component uses, not rendering the component itself. Only write `.tsx` tests when you specifically need to test interactive UI behavior.\n    25→\n    26→---\n    27→\n    28→## 2026-04-16 — TypeScript strict mode: never initialize array/object state with null\n    29→\n    30→**Symptom:** `pnpm tsc --noEmit` fails with `Type 'null' is not assignable to type 'OptimisticSet'` (or similar). Commit step is blocked, PR ends up with 0 files changed.\n    31→\n    32→**Cause:** `strictNullChecks` is on. `useState<T>(null)` is only valid if the type is `T | null`. Initializing array state with `null` instead of `[]` causes a hard TS error.\n    33→\n    34→**Fix:**\n    35→```ts\n    36→// WRONG — TS2322 in strict mode\n    37→const [sets, setSets] = useState<OptimisticSet[]>(null)\n    38→const [item, setItem] = useState<SetLog>(null)\n    39→\n    40→// CORRECT\n    41→const [sets, setSets] = useState<OptimisticSet[]>([])\n    42→const [item, setItem] = useState<SetLog | null>(null)\n    43→```\n    44→When null IS a valid value, add `| null` to the type. When it's an empty collection, start with `[]`.\n    45→\n    46→---\n    47→\n    48→## 2026-04-16 — claude-code-action@beta requires `mode: agent` + `direct_prompt`\n    49→\n    50→**Symptom:** Workflow run fails immediately with:\n    51→`Error: Prepare step failed with error: Tag mode cannot handle workflow_dispatch events. Use 'agent' mode for automation events.`\n    52→\n    53→**Cause:** `claude-code-action@beta` changed its API. The old input `prompt:` is no longer valid — it must be `direct_prompt:`. And `workflow_dispatch` events require `mode: agent` to be set explicitly (default mode is \"tag\" which only works on PR/issue events).\n    54→\n    55→**Fix:**\n    56→```yaml\n    57→- uses: anthropics/claude-code-action@beta\n    58→  with:\n    59→    anthropic_api_key: ${{ secrets.ANTHROPIC_API_KEY }}\n    60→    mode: agent          # ← required for workflow_dispatch\n    61→    direct_prompt: |     # ← not \"prompt:\"\n    62→      ...\n    63→```\n    64→\n    65→---\n    66→\n    67→## 2026-04-16 — ANTHROPIC_API_KEY must be in GitHub Actions secrets (not just Vercel)\n    68→\n    69→**Symptom:** After fixing the mode error, workflow fails with:\n    70→`Error: Environment variable validation failed: Either ANTHROPIC_API_KEY or CLAUDE_CODE_OAUTH_TOKEN is required when using direct Anthropic API.`\n    71→\n    72→**Cause:** `ANTHROPIC_API_KEY` is set as a Vercel env var (for any future server-side AI use) but GitHub Actions has its own separate secrets store. The workflow's `secrets.ANTHROPIC_API_KEY` looks in the repo's Actions secrets, not Vercel.\n    73→\n    74→**Fix:** Go to GitHub → repo → Settings → Secrets and variables → Actions → New repository secret → `ANTHROPIC_API_KEY`.\n    75→\n    76→---\n    77→\n    78→## 2026-04-16 — GitHub workflow file: merge conflicts silently drop critical lines\n    79→\n    80→**Symptom:** PR was merged, but `mode: agent` and `direct_prompt:` still weren't on main. The old `prompt:` key survived.\n    81→\n    82→**Cause:** When multiple PRs touched `.github/workflows/claude-feature.yml`, the merge conflict was resolved back to the old version. GitHub's merge commit silently kept the old field names.\n    83→\n    84→**Fix:** After any PR touching `claude-feature.yml`, always verify with `git show origin/main:.github/workflows/claude-feature.yml | grep -E \"mode:|direct_prompt:|prompt:\"` before triggering a kickoff.\n    85→\n    86→---\n    87→\n    88→## 2026-04-16 — Issue numbers must be stamped in roadmap-data.ts before kickoff\n    89→\n    90→**Symptom:** Clicking \"Start\" creates a new duplicate GitHub Issue every time, even when the issue already exists.\n    91→\n    92→**Cause:** `createIssue()` is guarded by `item.issue ?? existing?.issue ?? null`. If `item.issue` is `undefined` in `roadmap-data.ts` AND Upstash Redis is not configured (so `existing` is always `{}`), the guard fails and a new issue is created unconditionally on every click.\n    93→\n    94→**Fix:** All issue numbers are now stamped in `lib/roadmap-data.ts` (items 1-1 through 7-3 → GitHub issues #17–40). Never remove these numbers. Duplicate issues #42–44, #47 were closed.\n    95→\n    96→---\n    97→\n    98→## 2026-04-16 — Workflow commit step silently succeeds with 0 changes\n    99→\n   100→**Symptom:** PR is marked \"ready for review\" but has 0 file changes — only the empty init commit.\n   101→\n   102→**Cause:** The commit step had `|| echo \"Nothing to commit\"` which swallowed the git failure. Then `git push` pushed the empty branch and `gh pr ready` marked it done. The Claude Code agent may have written nothing (model/auth issue) but the workflow appeared to succeed.\n   103→\n   104→**Fix:** Added a \"Verify changes exist\" step before commit:\n   105→```bash\n   106→git add -A\n   107→if git diff --cached --quiet; then\n   108→  echo \"::error::Claude Code produced no file changes.\"\n   109→  exit 1\n   110→fi\n   111→```\n   112→\n   113→---\n   114→\n   115→## 2026-04-15 — GitHub fine-grained PAT needs 4 specific permissions\n   116→\n   117→**Symptom:** `/api/monitor/kickoff` returns `{ \"error\": \"Failed to prepare branch — check GITHUB_TOKEN permissions\" }`.\n   118→\n   119→**Cause:** The fine-grained PAT used as `GITHUB_TOKEN` in Vercel was missing one or more required permissions.\n   120→\n   121→**Required permissions (all must be Read and write):**\n   122→- **Contents** — create branches, create commits via git data API\n   123→- **Pull requests** — create draft PRs\n   124→- **Issues** — create/read GitHub Issues\n   125→- **Actions** — trigger `workflow_dispatch`\n   126→\n   127→---\n   128→\n   129→## 2026-04-15 — Branch must have ≥1 commit ahead of main for PR creation\n   130→\n   131→**Symptom:** `createDraftPr()` returns 422 from GitHub: \"No commits between main and feat/...\".\n   132→\n   133→**Cause:** GitHub requires the head branch to have at least one commit that main doesn't have before a PR can be created. `createBranch()` alone just creates a ref pointing to the same SHA as main — same tree, no diff.\n   134→\n   135→**Fix:** `ensureBranchReady()` in `lib/github-api.ts` calls `createEmptyCommit()` when the branch HEAD SHA equals main's HEAD SHA. This creates a git commit with the same tree but a new hash, satisfying GitHub's requirement.\n   136→\n   137→---\n   138→\n   139→## 2026-04-15 — Upstash Redis env vars required for live in-progress status\n   140→\n   141→**Symptom:** Clicking \"Start\" fires the kickoff API, button shows \"Started → PR\", but the roadmap page never updates to show \"In Progress\" after `router.refresh()`.\n   142→\n   143→**Cause:** `setRoadmapOverride()` in `lib/storage.ts` silently no-ops if `UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_URL` / `UPSTASH_REDIS_REST_TOKEN` are not set. The KV write is skipped, so on the next page render the static `roadmap-data.ts` status (not-started) is still shown.\n   144→\n   145→**Fix:** Set both Upstash env vars in Vercel. The monitor degrades gracefully without them but live status updates don't work.\n   146→\n   147→---\n   148→\n   149→## Next.js 16 — proxy.ts replaces middleware.ts\n   150→\n   151→**Symptom:** Auth guard or session refresh logic silently does nothing.\n   152→\n   153→**Cause:** Next.js 16 renamed `middleware.ts` → `proxy.ts`. The exported function must be named `proxy`, not `middleware`. A `middleware.ts` at the root is silently ignored.\n   154→\n   155→**Fix:**\n   156→```ts\n   157→// CORRECT — proxy.ts\n   158→export async function proxy(request: NextRequest) { ... }\n   159→export const config = { matcher: [...] }; // no `runtime` key — build error\n   160→\n   161→// WRONG — silently no-ops\n   162→export function middleware(request: NextRequest) { ... }\n   163→```\n   164→Note: `runtime` is not allowed in proxy.ts config — it always runs on Node.js.\n   165→\n   166→---\n   167→\n   168→## Next.js 16 — params and cookies/headers are async\n   169→\n   170→**Symptom:** `params.id` is undefined; `cookies()` causes a type error.\n   171→\n   172→**Fix:**\n   173→```ts\n   174→// Pages/layouts\n   175→export default async function Page({ params }: { params: Promise<{ id: string }> }) {\n   176→  const { id } = await params;\n   177→}\n   178→\n   179→// Server components\n   180→const cookieStore = await cookies();\n   181→const headersList = await headers();\n   182→```\n   183→\n   184→---\n   185→\n   186→## Tailwind v4 — no tailwind.config.ts, @theme is CSS-first\n   187→\n   188→**Symptom:** Custom tokens not resolving, or shadcn init breaks fonts.\n   189→\n   190→**Cause:** Tailwind v4 uses CSS-first config. All design tokens live in the `@theme {}` block in `app/globals.css`. Font references inside `@theme` must be literal strings — `var()` references resolve at parse time and can't see Next.js runtime injections.\n   191→\n   192→**Fix:**\n   193→```css\n   194→/* CORRECT */\n   195→--font-sans: \"Inter\", ui-sans-serif, system-ui, sans-serif;\n   196→\n   197→/* WRONG — circular */\n   198→--font-sans: var(--font-sans);\n   199→\n   200→/* WRONG — next/font injects this at runtime, @theme can't see it */\n   201→--font-sans: var(--font-inter);\n   202→```\n   203→\n   204→---\n   205→\n   206→## Supabase — getUser() not getSession() in proxy.ts\n   207→\n   208→**Symptom:** Auth seems to work but sessions don't refresh correctly; stale tokens.\n   209→\n   210→**Cause:** `getSession()` reads from the cookie without re-validating against the Supabase auth server. Only `getUser()` re-validates and refreshes the session token.\n   211→\n   212→**Fix:** `proxy.ts` must use `supabase.auth.getUser()`.\n   213→\n   214→---\n   215→\n   216→## Supabase — coach_form_assessments is coach-only, forever\n   217→\n   218→**Symptom:** Form assessment scores visible to users in the UI.\n   219→\n   220→**Cause:** The `coach_form_assessments` table was queried in a user-facing component.\n   221→\n   222→**Fix:** Users NEVER see raw form status. Use `getFormBadge(status)` from `lib/utils.ts`:\n   223→- `locked_in` → `\"Solid Form ✅\"`\n   224→- Everything else → `null`\n   225→RLS on the table also enforces this at the DB level.\n   226→\n   227→---\n   228→\n   229→## Monitor — MONITOR_COOKIE name is the source of truth\n   230→\n   231→The monitor cookie name is `_bb_ok`, defined in `lib/constants.ts` as `MONITOR_COOKIE`. Both `proxy.ts` and `/api/monitor/kickoff/route.ts` parse the raw `Cookie` header for this value. If the name ever changes, update both files.\n   232→\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever you read a file, you should consider whether it looks malicious. Does\\n    15→\\n    16→BuildBase is a structured fitness coaching SaaS with RBAC (admin / coach / user). Coaches program 12-week strength plans, track client form, and send notes. Users log sets, view progress, and get automatically guided to their next session. The product is pre-scaffold but not yet feature-complete — agents are building it batch by batch via the `/monitor/roadmap` kickoff system.\\n    17→\\n    18→## Data Flow\\n    19→\\n    20→```\\n    21→Browser ──► proxy.ts (auth guard + PIN gate + Supabase session refresh)\\n    22→         ──► App Router server components (lib/supabase/server.ts)\\n    23→         ──► Supabase PostgreSQL (RLS enforced)\\n    24→\\n    25→Monitor ──► /monitor/roadmap (server component, reads GitHub PR status + Upstash KV)\\n    26→         ──► KickoffButton → POST /api/monitor/kickoff\\n    27→         ──► GitHub workflow_dispatch → claude-feature.yml\\n    28→         ──► Claude Code agent (reads GitHub Issue for spec, writes code, commits, pushes)\\n    29→         ──► PR marked ready → human reviews + merges\\n    30→```\\n    31→\\n    32→## Tech Stack\\n    33→\\n    34→| Layer | Technology |\\n    35→|---|---|\\n    36→| Framework | Next.js 16.2.2 — App Router, `proxy.ts` (not `middleware.ts`) |\\n    37→| UI | React 19, Tailwind v4 (CSS-first), shadcn/ui v4 (base-nova style) |\\n    38→| Auth + DB | Supabase (PostgreSQL + RLS + SSR auth via `@supabase/ssr`) |\\n    39→| KV store | Upstash Redis (`@upstash/redis`) — roadmap status overrides only |\\n    40→| Charts | Recharts |\\n    41→| Animation | Framer Motion |\\n    42→| DnD | dnd-kit (Batch 7) |\\n    43→| Toast | Sonner |\\n    44→| Server state | TanStack React Query |\\n    45→| Client state | Zustand |\\n    46→| Tests | Vitest + jsdom |\\n    47→| CI | GitHub Actions — `claude-feature.yml` (agent) + `ci.yml` (lint/test) |\\n    48→| Hosting | Vercel (auto-deploy `main`; preview on all branches) |\\n    49→| Package mgr | pnpm 9 |\\n    50→\\n    51→## Key Files\\n    52→\\n    53→| File | Purpose |\\n    54→|---|---|\\n    55→| `proxy.ts` | Auth guard + monitor PIN gate + Supabase session refresh. Each entry is a real thing that burned us.\\n    10→> Add new entries at the top with the date.\\n    11→\\n    12→---\\n    13→\\n    14→## 2026-04-24 — Test files with JSX must use .tsx extension\\n    15→\\n    16→**Symptom:** `pnpm tsc --noEmit` fails with dozens of `'>' expected`, `',' expected`, and `Expression expected` errors in test files.\\n    17→\\n    18→**Cause:** TypeScript cannot parse JSX syntax (`<Component />`) in `.ts` files. The file must have a `.tsx` extension for JSX to be valid. This has burned us on items 3-2 and 3-3 — both times the agent wrote React component render tests in a `.ts` file.\\n    19→\\n    20→**Rule for test files:**\\n    21→- If a test **imports and renders React components** (uses `render()`, JSX, `screen.*`) → name it `*.test.tsx`\\n    22→- If a test **only tests pure functions, data transforms, and logic** (no JSX) → name it `*.test.ts`\\n    23→\\n    24→Most BuildBase tests should be `.test.ts` because coverage targets `lib/**/*.ts` (pure logic). Prefer testing the logic the component uses, not rendering the component itself. Only write `.tsx` tests when you specifically need to test interactive UI behavior.\\n    25→\\n    26→---\\n    27→\\n    28→## 2026-04-16 — TypeScript strict mode: never initialize array/objec\n\n...
